info:Super Wing Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family

posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:During the May Day holiday, we stayed in two Super Wings twin-bed rooms for 3 days and 2 nights for 1,299 yuan per night. We were 2 adults, 2 children and 2 seniors. We included breakfast and dinner buffets. The overall experience was good. The children liked the theme layout very much. The big bathtubs in each room were the favorites of the children, and the elderly also said it was comfortable. The weather in Guangzhou during the May Day holiday was not hot, so the outdoor swimming pool was too cold to swim. The hot spring room was in the men's and women's locker rooms of the gym, which was relatively small. For me, my 3-year-old son and 6-year-old daughter, it was a bit embarrassing for my son to go to the men's room with his father. The hotel did not have a half-inclusive heated swimming pool (Emerald Hilton and Nansha Garden Hotel are suitable for parents and children). The activities in the garden such as feeding fish, children smashing golden eggs, and scientific experiments were all very good. The garden was not big and there was not much green space. The baked bread in the breakfast buffet is different every day, but the egg tarts, donuts, and waffles that are more popular with children are not available every day. In addition, pickled salmon, sirloin and smoked ham are actually placed in the buffet dinner instead of with the bread slices for breakfast. These two items are a bit strange. Even if the breakfast buffet is mediocre, the sashimi back cuts in the dinner buffet are really sufficient, and the snails are super big, which is still great. Lunch was eaten at Taoli Restaurant in the hotel at my own expense, and I felt that the products were great. There were two live singers in the buffet lobby at noon and in the evening, which was also amazing. A welcome cake dessert was given when checking in, and finally two Ledi school bags were given after discussing with the customer service lady, which was very popular with the two children.

msg:The room is large and well soundproofed. The front desk of the hotel arranged a non-smoking room for our family of three. The bathtub is huge. There are two TV sets in the room. There are quite a lot of lighting fixtures.

If you stay during the National Day, you can experience the exploration game for free, which is quite fun. In the end, you will get a small badge for completing the task.

The swimming pool and gym are quite large, and you can also see a place for taking pictures and diving in the swimming pool in the gym, which is quite special.

The overall service for 2 days and one night was quite good. Check-in and check-out were fast and efficient. This is a very good experience compared to my experiences in other hotels.

All the waiters here are very polite and communicate well with gentle voices. Originally if it was time to check out. In just 26 hours (we used points to check in 10 hotels in advance), the experience was considered full marks. As a result, I felt a little helpless during the buffet breakfast time the next day. My husband took two children to have a meal (because the room only included breakfast for two, and the child was just 120cm). After finishing the food for the first meal, there was still a sign on the table saying that he was eligible to eat. As a result, he had to pack it up when he came back. The insufferable customer eats. I finally found a second table, and when I went to get my meal again, I told the customer next to me that if there was a waiter to collect the tableware, he would help me (and there was a sign saying "dining" again), and when I came back, he returned the order from the next table. I packed it up quickly before I could say anything. When I came back, I didn't know what to do with the food in my hands.

Regarding this, I understand very well. There are many people on holidays and the waiters are overwhelmed. I want to pack things up quickly and try to serve the most customers. But at the same time, my experience has been in other itineraries where there are so many people, and there are even more people than this time. It has never happened like this. The waiter is fast and there is no problem, but it is not possible to ask. At the next table? My child may not always be able to get hot food by herself. As a parent, I don‚Äôt trust her to get it by herself when there are many people. What if there are too many people and she gets hit? What about hitting food? Due to comprehensive considerations, only two people can pick up the meal. What if you put down your personal belongings? I feel that when the waiter is so busy, he may not notice it. Maybe he thinks that the guest has left something behind, and he is having breakfast instead of carrying a backpack? What should I bring for breakfast? So I was puzzled about this matter, and it took me a week to comment. This is the experience when the room rate includes a buffet, so I am glad that I did not go out and pay for an extra meal to experience this feeling. Therefore, please forgive me for my complete inability to make a reasonable and rational evaluation of the type of food, taste, environmental experience, etc.
